Func CONGXUONGMEOMAY()
	GUICtrlSetData($CRACK, "25")
	; Gửi combo chỉ 1 lần ở đầu
	If Not $g_bComboSent Then
		_SendComboOnce()
	EndIf
	Local $start = TimerInit()
	While TimerDiff($start) < 1
		_MEMORYPOINTERWRITE($FINALADDRESS, $HMEMORY, $OFFSET1, "1077979203")
		_MEMORYPOINTERWRITE($FINALADDRESS, $HMEMORY, $OFFSET2, "3224409287")
		_MEMORYPOINTERWRITE($FINALADDRESS, $HMEMORY, $OFFSET3, "1070176665")
	WEnd
